* The usage of this file is free of charge
* Freely share this for any kind of general aviation purposes including commercial devices such as planning tools, IGC loggers, navigation devices ect.
* Updates are released on regular basis on page https://www.aeroklub.cz/vzdusny-prostor/

* This file contains all CZ DROPZONE airfields


****************************************
***** LKAA DROPZONES (Dangerous Areas) ******
****************************************

*Setting colour and line of Danger (Q) airspace
AC Q
SP 0,2,127,0,127
SB -1,-1,-1


*AC Q
*AN DROPZONE 
*AF 
*AH FL 95
*AL 0 AGL
*V X=
*DC 2 *NM
